shared_focus = {
	id = ENG_passing_king

	icon = GFX_ENG_the_king_passes
	x = 9
	y = 0
	offset = {
		x = 0
		y = 0
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = ENG_attlee_labour_tree
				has_country_flag = ENG_butler_conservative_tree
			}
		}
	}
	offset = {
		x = -9
		y = 0
		trigger = {
			has_focus_tree = british_focus_mac
		}
	}
	offset = {
		x = -9
		y = 0
		trigger = {
			has_focus_tree = british_focus_butler_second

		}
	}

	cost = 1

	ai_will_do = {
		base = 0
	}

	available = {
		custom_trigger_tooltip = {
			tooltip = always_available_no
			always = no
		}
	}
	available_if_capitulated = no

	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus ENG_passing_king"
		custom_effect_tooltip = ENG_passing_king_tt
	}
}

		}

			value = 0.1
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = ENG_inflation_increase_0.1
		add_timed_idea = { idea = ENG_nhs_boost days = 1000 }
		country_event = { id = twrbritainflavour.37 hours = 0 }
	}
}

			name = motorised_bonus

			uses = 1

		}

	            var = ENG_balance_of_payments_var
	            value = 0.1
	        }
		}
	}
}

	}

		}
	}

	available = {
		date > 1957.01.01
	}

	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus ENG_new_election_conservative"
		# start the election campaign thing again
		set_country_flag = ENG_2nd_election_con
		activate_mission = SECOND_CONS_time_left
		custom_effect_tooltip = ENG_new_election_tt
		country_event = { id = twrbritainpolitics.400 hours = 0 }
		hidden_effect = {
			clamp_variable = {
				var = ENG_labour_poll
				min = 0
				max = ENG_COMMONS_total_seat
			}
			clamp_variable = {
				var = ENG_conservative_poll
				min = 0
				max = ENG_COMMONS_total_seat
			}
			clamp_variable = {
				var = ENG_liberal_poll
				min = 0
				max = ENG_COMMONS_total_seat
			}
			clamp_variable = {
				var = ENG_independent_poll
				min = 0
				max = ENG_COMMONS_total_seat
			}
			set_variable = { ENG_labour_poll = 311 }
			set_variable = { ENG_conservative_poll = 291 }
			set_variable = { ENG_liberal_poll = 20 }
			set_variable = { ENG_independent_poll = 3 }
			set_variable = { ENG_COMMONS_total_seat = 625 }
		}
	}

shared_focus = {
	id = ENG_new_elections_con_lib
	icon = GFX_ENG_elections
	prerequisite = { focus = ENG_amicable_breakup_con_lib }

	x = 0
	y = 11
	relative_position_id = ENG_hung_parliament

	cost = 8

	ai_will_do = {
		base = 20
	}
	available = {
	NOT = { has_country_flag = ENG_2ND_ELECTION_COMPLETE }
	}
	available = {
		date > 1957.01.01
	}

	available_if_capitulated = no

	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus ENG_new_elections_con_lib"
		# add stuff for 2nd election #
		set_country_flag = ENG_2nd_election_con
		activate_mission = SECOND_CONS_time_left
		custom_effect_tooltip = ENG_new_election_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			clamp_variable = {
				var = ENG_labour_poll
				min = 0
				max = ENG_COMMONS_total_seat
			}
			clamp_variable = {
				var = ENG_conservative_poll
				min = 0
				max = ENG_COMMONS_total_seat
			}
			clamp_variable = {
				var = ENG_liberal_poll
				min = 0
				max = ENG_COMMONS_total_seat
			}
			clamp_variable = {
				var = ENG_independent_poll
				min = 0
				max = ENG_COMMONS_total_seat
			}
			set_variable = { ENG_labour_poll = 311 }
			set_variable = { ENG_conservative_poll = 291 }
			set_variable = { ENG_liberal_poll = 20 }
			set_variable = { ENG_independent_poll = 3 }
			set_variable = { ENG_COMMONS_total_seat = 625 }
			# added this
		}
	}
}
